   function getGeoCode(){
      var req = new XMLHttpRequest();
      req.open("GET", '/check-geo-country', false);
      req.send(null);
      var gcode = req.getResponseHeader("x-geo-country");
      return (gcode) ? gcode.toLowerCase() : "us";
    }
